            한국어-대한민국 [ko-KR] 🇰🇷</option></select><select name="time_range" id="time_range" class="time_range" aria-label="Time range"><option id="time-range-anytime" value="" selected>Anytime</option><option id="time-range-day" value="day" >Last day</option><option id="time-range-week" value="week" >Last week</option><option id="time-range-month" value="month" >Last month</option><option id="time-range-year" value="year" >Last year</option></select><select  name="safesearch" id="safesearch" class="safesearch" aria-label="SafeSearch">
